function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 67') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.67!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// Dir added: links
@mkdir('links');
if (!is_dir('links')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: links');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('links', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of links');
}

// File added: links/ViaThinkSoft.url
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('links/ViaThinkSoft.url', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('W3swMDAyMTRBMC0wMDAwLTAwMDAtQzAwMC0wMDAwMDAwMDAwNDZ9XQpQcm9wMz0xOSwyCltJbnRlcm5ldFNob3J0Y3V0XQpVUkw9aHR0cDovL3d3dy52aWF0aGlua3NvZnQuY29tLwpJRExpc3Q9Cgo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('links/ViaThinkSoft.url') && (sha1_file('links/ViaThinkSoft.url') != '0a68fad4282aa246b245bd1d34278c864063fe27')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: links/ViaThinkSoft.url');
	$tmp = pathinfo('links/ViaThinkSoft.url');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('links/ViaThinkSoft.url')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('links/ViaThinkSoft.url', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('links/ViaThinkSoft.url')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): links/ViaThinkSoft.url');
} else if (sha1_file('links/ViaThinkSoft.url') != '0a68fad4282aa246b245bd1d34278c864063fe27') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): links/ViaThinkSoft.url');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('links/ViaThinkSoft.url', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of links/ViaThinkSoft.url');
}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}

}

	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php') != '659ea7e3bdc91e19d914c6cebde2873da7965613') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php') !== '659ea7e3bdc91e19d914c6cebde2873da7965613') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php') !== '659ea7e3bdc91e19d914c6cebde2873da7965613') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusObject.class.php');

	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') != '2d82c197063bbaea9c81ad9f2ea743b707b14f86') {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== '2d82c197063bbaea9c81ad9f2ea743b707b14f86') {

if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.js');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != 'd45f7543d3af214efd3befaff53f4fd29cdad463') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== 'd45f7543d3af214efd3befaff53f4fd29cdad463') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '171c624efe53bc8dcd082aaa9cf50ac6d1b923ea') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== 'd45f7543d3af214efd3befaff53f4fd29cdad463') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
		}
	}
}

	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php') != '5bd4f8640f6f7f5fad44e9a2a1d7055cefcc0853') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php') !== '5bd4f8640f6f7f5fad44e9a2a1d7055cefcc0853') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php') !== '683bdc4eba16be1309f65d970e495f3cc9deefe4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php') !== '5bd4f8640f6f7f5fad44e9a2a1d7055cefcc0853') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/500_documents/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 68\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 68') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
